02/06/22, 23:34 - Ramakant Tiwari: Does Including more header file affect program speed in C Programming?
02/06/22, 23:34 - Ramakant Tiwari: Hard to be 100% sure, but logically it shouldn‚Äôt make any difference.

If you include a header file and don‚Äôt use anything from it, the code may or may not be linked and compiled (depending on the compiler), but once the program is running it will just sit there and never be called, so while the program may compile a bit slower, and the binary be a bit bigger, it should run at just the same speed as before.

If you actually need something from the header, then not including it means you‚Äôll presumably have to write whatever it is from scratch. Whether your version will be faster or slower than the library version depends on many things, but let‚Äôs just assume it runs the same speed. In that case, your program will take longer to write without the header, will probably compile and link a bit faster and have a smaller binary, but will run at the same speed.

int prime(int x)
{
    int i;
    for(i=2;i<=x-1;i++)
    {
        if(x%i==0)
            break;
    }
    if(x==i)
        return x;

}

#include<math.h>  
  
int main()  
{  
    int num, count, i, prime;  
  
    printf("Prime Numbers from 1 To 500 are\n");  
  
    for(num = 1; num <= 500; num++)  
    {  
        if(num == 1)  
        {  
            printf("Number 1 is neither prime nor composite\n");  
            continue;  
        }  
  
        count = sqrt(num);  
        prime = 1;  
        for(i = 2; i <= count; i++)  
        {  
            if(num % i == 0)  
            {  
                prime = 0;  
                break;  
            }  
        }  
  
        if(prime)  
        {  
            printf("%d\t", num);  
        }  
    }  
  
    return 0;  
}

05/06/22, 00:21 - Ramakant Tiwari: #include <stdio.h>
void main()
{
    int match_stickes = 21;
    int player, computer;
    while (1)
    {
        printf("Total Number of Match sticks : %d\n", match_stickes);
        printf("Pick from 1 to 4 matches\n");
        scanf("%d", &player);
        if (player < 1 || player > 4)
            continue;
        match_stickes -= player;
        printf("Match Stickes left after your pickup : %d\n", match_stickes);
        computer = 5 - player;
        printf("No. of match stickes Computer picked: %d\n", computer);
        match_stickes -= computer;
        if (match_stickes == 1)
        {
            printf("Only 1 Match Stick left.\nYou lost the game!\n");
            break;
        }
    }
}

‚Äì Whoever is forced to pick up the last matchstick loses the game.

void main()
{
    int num;
    char ans;
    int positive = 0, negative = 0, zero = 0;
    do
    {
        printf("ENTER A NUMBER TO CHECK WHETHER IT'S EVEN, ODD OR ZERO\n");
        scanf("%d", &num);
        if (num > 0)
            positive++;
        else if (num < 0)
            negative++;
        else
            zero++;
        printf("WANT TO CHECK MORE NUMBERS?(Y for YES and N for NO)?\n");
        
        scanf("%c", &ans); //FOR ANSWER
        
    } while(ans == 'Y' || ans == 'y');
    printf("TOTAL NUMBER OF POSITIVE NUMBERS: %d\n", positive);
    printf("TOTAL NUMBER OF NEGATIVE NUMBERS: %d\n", negative);
    printf("TOTAL NUMBER OF ZEROES: %d\n", zero);
}

20/07/22, 23:55 - Ramakant Tiwari: #include<stdio.h>
void main() {
    int arr[5], num;
    void scanArray(int[],int); void printArray(int[],int); void insertion(int[],int);

    num = sizeof(arr)/sizeof(arr[0]);

    printf("Enter array elememts:\n");
    scanArray(arr, num);

    printf("The Array is: ");
    printArray(arr, num);

    insertion(arr, num);
}

void scanArray(int arr[], int num){
    for(int i=0;i<num;i++)
    scanf("%d",&arr[i]);
}

void printArray(int arr[], int num) {
    for(int i=0;i<num;i++)
    printf("%d ",arr[i]);
}

void insertion(int arr[],int num){
    for(int counter=0;counter<(num-1);counter++){
    int key = arr[counter+1];
    while(key<arr[counter] && counter >= 0){
        arr[counter+1]=arr[counter];
        counter--; 
    }
    arr[counter+1] = key;
    }

    printf("\nThe Sorted Array is: ");
    printArray(arr, num);
}

void main()
{
    int input, terms, numerator, denominator;
    float sum = 0;
    int func1(int, int);
    int func2(int);
    printf("Input the value of x : ");
    scanf("%d", &input);
    printf("Input number of terms : ");
    scanf("%d", &terms);
    for (int i = 0; i <= terms; ++i)
    {
        numerator = func1(input, i);
        denominator = func2(i);
        sum += ((float)numerator / (float)denominator);
        printf("%d/%d + ", numerator, denominator);
    }
    printf("\nThe sum is %f\n", sum);
}
int func1(int base, int exponent)
{
    int value = 1;
    for (int i = 1; i <= exponent; ++i)
    {
        value *= base;
    }
    return value;
}
int func2(int limit)
{
    int fact = 1;
    for (int i = 1; i <= limit; ++i)
    {
        fact *= i;
    }
    return fact;
}

using namespace std;

string ltrim(const string &);
string rtrim(const string &);
vector<string> split(const string &);



/*
* Complete the 'findLargestSquareSize' function below.
*
* The function is expected to return an INTEGER.
* The function accepts 2D_INTEGER_ARRAY samples as parameter.
*/

int findLargestSquareSize(vector<vector<int>> samples) {
int _res = 0;
int _row = samples.size();
int _col = samples[0].size();
vector <vector <int>> matrix(_row, vector<int>(_col,0));
int x, y;
for(x=0; x < _row; ++x)
{
for(y=0; y < _col; y++)
{
if(x==0||y==0)
{
if(samples[x][y] ==1)
matrix[x][y] = 1;
}
else {
if (samples[x][y] ==1)
matrix[x][y] = min(matrix[x-1][y],min(matrix[x][y-1],matrix[x-1][y-1])) + 1;
}
_res = max(_res,matrix[x][y]);
}
}
return _res ;
}

int main()
{
ofstream fout(getenv("OUTPUT_PATH"));

string samples_rows_temp;
getline(cin, samples_rows_temp);

int samples_rows = stoi(ltrim(rtrim(samples_rows_temp)));

string samples_columns_temp;
getline(cin, samples_columns_temp);

int samples_columns = stoi(ltrim(rtrim(samples_columns_temp)));

vector<vector<int>> samples(samples_rows);

for (int i = 0; i < samples_rows; i++) {
samples[i].resize(samples_columns);

string samples_row_temp_temp;
getline(cin, samples_row_temp_temp);

vector<string> samples_row_temp = split(rtrim(samples_row_temp_temp));

for (int j = 0; j < samples_columns; j++) {
int samples_row_item = stoi(samples_row_temp[j]);

samples[i][j] = samples_row_item;
}
}

int result = findLargestSquareSize(samples);

fout << result << "\n";

fout.close();

return 0;
}

string ltrim(const string &str) {
string s(str);

s.erase(
s.begin(),
find_if(s.begin(), s.end(), not1(ptr_fun<int, int>(isspace)))
);

return s;
}

string rtrim(const string &str) {
string s(str);

s.erase(
find_if(s.rbegin(), s.rend(), not1(ptr_fun<int, int>(isspace))).base(),
s.end()
);

return s;
}

vector<string> split(const string &str) {
vector<string> tokens;

string::size_type start = 0;
string::size_type end = 0;

while ((end = str.find(" ", start)) != string::npos) {
tokens.push_back(str.substr(start, end - start));

start = end + 1;
}

tokens.push_back(str.substr(start));

return tokens;
}

22/08/22, 18:18 - Ramakant Tiwari: #include <bits/stdc++.h>

using namespace std;

string ltrim(const string &);
string rtrim(const string &);


/*
* Complete the 'getOneBits' function below.
*
* The function is expected to return an INTEGER_ARRAY.
* The function accepts INTEGER n as parameter.
*/

vector<int> getOneBits(int n) {
vector <int> vee;
vector <int> aar;
int X, Y, Z=0;
while(n!=0)
{
X = n % 2;
vee.push_back(X);
n /= 2;
}
reverse(vee.begin(), vee.end());
for(Y = 0; Y < vee.size(); ++Y)
{
if(vee[Y] == 1)
{
++Z;
}
}
aar.push_back(Z);
for(Y = 0; Y < vee.size(); ++Y)
{
if(vee[Y] == 1)
{
aar.push_back(Y+1);
}
}
return aar;
}
int main()
{
ofstream fout(getenv("OUTPUT_PATH"));

string n_temp;
getline(cin, n_temp);

int n = stoi(ltrim(rtrim(n_temp)));

vector<int> result = getOneBits(n);

for (size_t i = 0; i < result.size(); i++) {
fout << result[i];

if (i != result.size() - 1) {
fout << "\n";
}
}

fout << "\n";

fout.close();

return 0;
}

);

s.end()
);

29/09/22, 22:19 - Ramakant Tiwari: You are given S, a sequence of n integers i.e. S = s1, s2, ..., sn. Compute if it is possible to split S into two parts : s1, s2, ..., si and si+1, si+2, ‚Ä¶.., sn (0 <= i <= n) in such a way that the first part is strictly decreasing while the second is strictly increasing one.
Note : We say that x is strictly larger than y when x > y.
So, a strictly increasing sequence can be 1 4 8. However, 1 4 4 is NOT a strictly increasing sequence.


That is, in the sequence if numbers are decreasing, they can start increasing at one point. And once the sequence of numbers starts increasing, they cannot decrease at any point further.
Sequence made up of only increasing numbers or only decreasing numbers is a valid sequence. So, in both the cases, print true.

11/11/22, 23:19 - Ramakant Tiwari: #include <iostream>
using namespace std;


void merging(int a1[], int n1, int a2[], int n2, int arr[], int size) {
	int i = 0, j = 0, k = 0;
	while(i < n1 && j < n2) {
		if(a1[i] < a2[j]) arr[k++] = a1[i++];
		else arr[k++] = a2[j++];
	}
	if(i <= n1) {
		while(j < n2) 
			arr[k++] = a2[j++];
	}
	else {
		while(i < n1) 
			arr[k++] = a1[i++];
	}	
}

void mergeSort(int input[], int size){
	// Write your code here
	if(size > 1) {
		int n1 = size / 2;
		int n2 = size - n1;
		int *a1 = new int[n1];
		int *a2 = new int[n2];
		for(int i = 0; i < n1; i++) a1[i] = input[i];
		for(int i = 0; i < n2; i++) a2[i] = input[n1 + i];
		mergeSort(a1, n1);
		mergeSort(a2, n2);
		merging(a1, n1, a2, n2, input, size);
	}
}


int main() {
	int length;
	cin >> length;
	int* input = new int[length];
	for(int i=0; i < length; i++)
		cin >> input[i];
	mergeSort(input, length);
	for(int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
		cout << input[i] << " ";
	}
}

30/01/23, 08:47 - Ramakant Tiwari: #include <iostream>
#include <string>
#include <vector>
using namespace std;

class TrieNode {
   public:
    char data;
    TrieNode **children;
    bool isTerminal;

    TrieNode(char data) {
        this->data = data;
        children = new TrieNode *[26];
        for (int i = 0; i < 26; i++) {
            children[i] = NULL;
        }
        isTerminal = false;
    }
};

class Trie {
    TrieNode *root;

   public:
    int count;

    Trie() {
        this->count = 0;
        root = new TrieNode('\0');
    }

    bool insertWord(TrieNode *root, string word) {
        // Base case
        if (word.size() == 0) {
            if (!root->isTerminal) {
                root->isTerminal = true;
                return true;
            } else {
                return false;
            }
        }

        // Small calculation
        int index = word[0] - 'a';
        TrieNode *child;

        if (root->children[index] != NULL) {
            child = root->children[index];
        } else {
            child = new TrieNode(word[0]);
            root->children[index] = child;
        }

        // Recursive call
        return insertWord(child, word.substr(1));
    }

    void insertWord(string word) {
        if (insertWord(root, word)) {
            this->count++;
        }
    }

    void autoComplete(vector<string> input, string pattern) {
        // Write your code here
    }
};

int main() {
    Trie t;
    int n;
    cin >> n;

    vector<string> vect;

    for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i) {
        string word;
        cin >> word;
        vect.push_back(word);
    }

    string pattern;
    cin >> pattern;

    t.autoComplete(vect, pattern);
}

12/02/23, 19:09 - Ramakant Tiwari: find all ways to construct target from wordbank. 
target - abcdef
wordbank - [ab, abc, cd, def, abcd, ef, c]

output - [[ab, cd, ef], [ab, c, def], [abc, def], [abcd, ef]]

#include <bits/stdc++.h>
using namespace std;

unordered_map<string, vector<vector<string>>> output;
vector<vector<string>> allConstruct(string target, vector<string> wordBank) {
  if (output.count(target)) {
    return output[target];
  }

  if (target.empty()) {
    vector<vector<string>> str;
    return str;
  }

  vector<vector<string>> result;
  for (int i = 0; i < wordBank.size(); i++) {
    string word = wordBank[i];

    if (target.find(word) == 0) {
      string suffix = target.substr(word.size());
      vector<vector<string>> suffixWays = allConstruct(suffix, wordBank);

      vector<vector<string>> targetWays;
      for (int i = 0; i < suffixWays.size(); i++) {
        vector<string> temp = suffixWays.at(i);
        temp.push_back(word);
        targetWays.push_back(temp);
      }

      for (int i = 0; i < targetWays.size(); i++) {
        result.push_back(targetWays[i]);
      }
    }
  }

  output[target] = result;
  return output[target];
}

int main() {
  string s;
  cin >> s;
  vector<string> vect;
  int n;
  cin >> n;
  while (n--) {
    string data;
    cin >> data;
    vect.push_back(data);
  }

  vector<vector<string>> ans = allConstruct(s, vect);
  for (int i = 0; i < ans.size(); i++) {
    for (int j = 0; j < ans.at(i).size(); j++) {
      cout << ans.at(i).at(j) << " ";
    }
    cout << endl;
  }
}

    <script>
        alert("Welcome to THE GUESSING NUMBER GAME");
        alert("Shaho and Vincent you both have to guess a number in range(1-10)");
        let shahoGuesses = [], vincentGuesses = [], randomNum = [];
        while (true) {
            const min = 1, max = 10;
            const numToGuess = Math.floor(Math.random() * (max - min) + min);
            randomNum.push(numToGuess);
            const shaho = parseInt(prompt("Shaho turn"));
            shahoGuesses.push(shaho);
            if (shaho === numToGuess) {
                alert(`Shaho Won.\nRandom Numbers: ${randomNum}\nHis guesses: ${shahoGuesses}.`);
                break;
            }
            const vincent = parseInt(prompt("Vincent turn"));
            vincentGuesses.push(vincent);
            if (vincent === numToGuess) {
                alert(`Vincent Won.\nRandom Numbers: ${randomNum}\nHis guesses: ${vincentGuesses}.`);
                break;
            }
        }
    </script>
